  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_83392df7-72ad-4808-9477-3592fca868e4'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer1971255988198551414">Sam Parker is a vampire with a gift so strong and substantial that she is invited to partake in a test for a place in the Grand High Master Vampire’s private army. She finds that not only has the army never included a woman, but it has never included a Sventé vampire; a breed that is regarded by the super strong Pagori breed and the hypnotically beautiful Keja breed to be </span>
  <span id="freeText1971255988198551414" style="display:none">Sam Parker is a vampire with a gift so strong and substantial that she is invited to partake in a test for a place in the Grand High Master Vampire’s private army. She finds that not only has the army never included a woman, but it has never included a Sventé vampire; a breed that is regarded by the super strong Pagori breed and the hypnotically beautiful Keja breed to be too tame and human-like. Most refuse to take her seriously, especially a Pagori commander named Jared who she craves in spite of herself.<br /><br />The Grand High Master, however, sees her potential and offers her the position of Jared’s co-commander to help train the newest squad in time for the impending attack on his home. Sam has to demonstrate to Jared and the squad of chauvinists why it is incredibly foolish to underestimate a wilful, temperamental, borderline-homicidal Sventé female. <br /><br />Warning: This novel contains an iron-willed female vampire with an energy whip, a sexist male vampire who is determined to have her, explicit vampy sex, and a romance story with real bite.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1971255988198551414" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1246460598" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1246460598?book_show_action=true">Apr 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-p-z">authors-p-z</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=humour">humour</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=vampire-shapeshifters">vampire-shapeshifters</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1246460598" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7658203597296786882"><blockquote>
  
    <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410813339ra/11155618.gif' alt=' photo sofreakinexcited_zps32f56db3.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</blockquote>I am so excited!!! I just discovered a new vampire series!!! And I am beyond thrilled!!!<br/><br/>Suzanne Wright has created the most exciting and yes, different world of vampires in her Deep in Your Veins Series.<br/><br/>Three different kinds of vampires, ….and each vampire with their very own special powers.<blockquote>
  <b> “Three breeds? Well you see, basically, you know how there are varying accounts of vampires? Some humans report us to be terribly aggressive with hulk-like strength, some report us to be entra</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText7658203597296786882" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410813339ra/11155618.gif" alt=" photo sofreakinexcited_zps32f56db3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>I am so excited!!! I just discovered a new vampire series!!! And I am beyond thrilled!!!<br><br>Suzanne Wright has created the most exciting and yes, different world of vampires in her Deep in Your Veins Series.<br><br>Three different kinds of vampires, ….and each vampire with their very own special powers.<blockquote>
  <b> “Three breeds? Well you see, basically, you know how there are varying accounts of vampires? Some humans report us to be terribly aggressive with hulk-like strength, some report us to be entrancingly beautiful and charming, and others believe that we are actually more human-like than the stories say. Well the reason for all the confusion is that there are actually different breeds.”</b>
</blockquote>The first book in the series, Here Be Sexist Vampires takes us into a world filled with gorgeous, sexy, mysterious and very very likeable characters.<br><br>Samantha aka Sam is a London vampire, one of the lowest ranking vampire groups. <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428251096i/14395216.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_n3bl5u6Uze1r8hms0_zps8o9ti5uz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>She joins Cat from Night Huntress series by Jeaniene Frost and Merit from Chicagoland Vampires by Chloe Neill as my three top kickass and fabulous vampire heroines.<br><br>Sam is such an incredible and funny character. She takes no shit from anyone. She’s smart and quick on the uptake. Underneath all that smarty pants is someone with a vulnerable side…someone who has been abused, seen and done some scary things in her life, and who has suffered loss and pain – but she does not let that stand in her way.<blockquote>
  <b>"I’ve done things in my time that would make the curly hairs in your pants go straight,female or not, I reckon i’ve got bigger balls than you have"</b>
</blockquote>When she’s offered a job working for Antonio, the Master of all Vampires, she sees this as the way to get away from Viktor, her tormentor and the vampire who turned her and has kept her prisoner since.<br><br>Arriving at Antonio’s compound, she’s given the position of commander of the new vampire recruits, together with Jared, Antonio’s heir and a total sexist and arrogant and gorgeous vampire of the highest ranking. Wow, does this guy think a lot about himself…<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428251096ra/14395217.gif" alt=" photo ian-somerhalder-tvd-Favim.com-369717_zpssbti8mnn.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>And he’s a total slut….has 3 consorts and just screws around!! <blockquote>
  <b>"Men! if he was a women he’d be considered a bit of a slut but apparently because he was a male it was completely normal and acceptable."</b>
</blockquote> He actually thinks that Sam will give in to his sexiness….but man has he made a mistake in thinking that she’s just a girl….oh did I forget to mention that Sam is the only female vampire ever to work with the legion vampire army!!! She certainly knows how to put a dolt like him in place…<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428251096ra/14395218.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_n3bn1poV3L1r8hms0_zpsyaiofnth.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> I loved the characters in this book. Sam’s vampire group, Antonio, Luther, Sebastian, Jared’s 3 consorts (talk about princesses….)and most of all, I fell in love with Sam’s PA, Fletcher…..totally lovable and adorable…<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428251096i/14395219.jpg" alt=" photo marc_l_zpshybazdkt.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> I want a Fletcher of my own!!!! He’s such an unforgettable and engaging character and I can’t get enough of him.<br><br>I liked the interaction, sexual tension and chemistry between Sam &amp; Jared and loved watching the build-up of the attraction that they felt for each other. <blockquote>
  <b> “God, I loved this woman: this very crazy, borderline-homicidal – on second thought, scrap the borderline – woman.” <br><br>“How could you be attracted to someone who made you so pissed off that you’d considered burning their balls with a lighter?”</b>
</blockquote><br>Another thing about this series that I totally love is the writing and the dialogue. <blockquote>
  <b>"What? Who? Oh you mean that cross between a whippet and witch personally. I don’t know how he can shag something that looks like it’s just escaped from Azkaban."</b>
</blockquote>The author is British and the humour and wit come across each page. Sam’s vocabulary is a total blast….<br><blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428251096ra/14395220.gif" alt=" photo giphy_zpsxwfepa1l.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> Hilarious and so fabulous….<blockquote>
  <b> He had to be blowing smoke up my arse.</b>
</blockquote> Okay there are some OTT moments and characters that are just so out there…..but that’s the magic in writing..anything is possible! <br><br>The funniest vampire book I have ever read…just loved it!!!<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428251096ra/14395221.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_n3bnitpH4g1r8hms0_zpsx1nlem19.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>Can’t wait to start book #2…..and join Sam &amp; Jared on their next vampiric adventure!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7658203597296786882" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer488009564" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17838597043665299327"><i>6 who's your mama stars</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412640054i/11400420.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Sam</u>
</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Female or not, I reckon I’ve got bigger balls than you have.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412640054i/11400421._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Vampire Breed:</b> Sventé - tame and human-like<br/><b>Special Gift:</b> Feeder<br/><b>Previous Employment:</b> Chief Assassin<br/><b>Favorite weapon:</b> <i>"Bolts, beams, balls, but I like the whip best. It’s more fun...and natural energies, the classical elements; air, water, fire and earth.”</i><br/><b>Goal:</b> To finally be free of her Sire, Victor, by any means necessary<br/><b>Best Described as:</b> <i>"very crazy, borderline-homicidal – on second thought, s</i></span>
  <span id="freeText17838597043665299327" style="display:none"><i>6 who's your mama stars</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412640054i/11400420.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Sam</u>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Female or not, I reckon I’ve got bigger balls than you have.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412640054i/11400421._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Vampire Breed:</b> Sventé - tame and human-like<br><b>Special Gift:</b> Feeder<br><b>Previous Employment:</b> Chief Assassin<br><b>Favorite weapon:</b> <i>"Bolts, beams, balls, but I like the whip best. It’s more fun...and natural energies, the classical elements; air, water, fire and earth.”</i><br><b>Goal:</b> To finally be free of her Sire, Victor, by any means necessary<br><b>Best Described as:</b> <i>"very crazy, borderline-homicidal – on second thought, scrap the borderline – woman."</i><br><br>Sam is the first female Sventé Feeder who has tremendous control over her gift, leaving everyone who comes across her stunned and usually laying flat on their ass. She gets offered a chance to try-out to join the Grand High Master Vampire’s private army and in return a chance to finally be free of her Sire, Victor, of three years. Willing to take the risk of his wrath, she has no other option if she ever wants to no longer be his <i>hostage, sex slave and assassin.</i> <br><br><b>
  <u>Jared</u>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“So you’re prejudiced against women, young vampires, and against another breed of vampire. I bet you’re a delight to have around.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412640054i/11400422._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Vampire Breed:</b> Pagori - super strong <br><b>Special Gift:</b> Electrokinetic and Telepathy<br><b>Current Employment:</b> Commander of the Grand High Master Vampire’s private army &amp; Heir of the Grand High Master<br><b>Favorite weapon:</b> high voltage electricity<br><b>Goal:</b> To train and lead the strongest army against the impending attack on the Grand High Master<br><b>Best Described as:</b> protective, demanding, controlling and master lover<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412640054ra/11400423.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jared is the best of the best, that is why he holds the position he does today, but when Sam comes into his squad to try-out he wants to prove to her that only real men can handle being a part of his squad. He has no clue as to why Antonio would have offered Sam a position as a co-commander after he refused to select her as part of the squad. It was nothing personal, she just wouldn't be a good fit for the squad. <br><br>Isolated on an island Antonio, the Grand High Master, selects those he trusts dear to be around him. One of his trusted adviser's, Luther, had a vision of an impending attack on the island, and determines it necessary that the new squad be trained and ready in the weeks to come. Sam is no stranger to hard work, she knows she cannot just demand respect...she will need to prove it to this squad of chauvinists pigs. And so help her God she doesn't cause bodily harm to any of them, especially the main pig himself, Jared. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>How could you be attracted to someone who made you so pissed off that you’d considered burning their balls with a lighter?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412640054ra/11400424.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sam is pissed off at herself for letting Jared get the best of her, why should she care how many consorts he has. Why should she care what he thinks especially now that she finally has the freedom from her Sire and a place to call home. As much as they try to ignore each other, there is no stop to the insults and the constant conflict...it's all just foreplay for these two, and it's only a matter of time before the fire ignites and the inevitable occurs, when the two become one the battle of the bedroom begins. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Jared’s lips were suddenly at my ear. “The only vampire who’ll be manhandling you tonight is me.” <br><br>“If I let you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412640149ra/11400456.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Here Be Sexist Vampire</b> is an amazing funny sexy tale, one I cannot believe I put aside for so long. Ms. Wright truly has a gift for creating a world you can live in with characters that you love or love to hate. Sam is a temperamental, strong-willed, sarcastic female who is a complete bad ass on and off the field. She will only submit to a deserving partner, after of course she makes him work for it. Jared was a strong alpha male lead, but he understood Sam and let her be who she needed to be no matter how much it drove him mad with concern. The back and forth banter between Sam and Jared and the rest of the squad kept me laughing and dying for more. <br><br>There is action, a little suspense and some sexy luvin too, what more could you possibly ask for. I had to admit I was kind of scared when I found out there was more books for Jared and Sam, but this can be read as a stand-alone as there is a sense of an ending and a promise of more if you continue. With these characters I had to jump right into the next book because I couldn't let go just yet, I was having way too much fin with them. Awesome read for sure and recommended to all my paranormal lover friends.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17838597043665299327" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_737074070" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/737074070" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/737074070?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17826184-here-be-sexist-vampires">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">PNR ADDICTS</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11963959-lisa?shelf=love-you-forever-and-ever">love-you-forever-and-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11963959-lisa?shelf=addicted-to-this-author">addicted-to-this-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer737074070" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15808297923879406615"><b>5 BITE ME STARS.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"... Well I love that sexist twat just because."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381396346i/4803091._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book is immediately hitting my love-you-forever-and ever-shelf, and in honor of this fantastic author a new shelf has been added; Addicted to this author. This book was a real honest to goodness, 'I don't want to put you down ever' page turner. I've had this book on my kindle for some time now and after feeling in the mood for a bit of paranormal loving I knew I could turn to this author and she would deliver and deliver sh</span>
  <span id="freeText15808297923879406615" style="display:none"><b>5 BITE ME STARS.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"... Well I love that sexist twat just because."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381396346i/4803091._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is immediately hitting my love-you-forever-and ever-shelf, and in honor of this fantastic author a new shelf has been added; Addicted to this author. This book was a real honest to goodness, 'I don't want to put you down ever' page turner. I've had this book on my kindle for some time now and after feeling in the mood for a bit of paranormal loving I knew I could turn to this author and she would deliver and deliver she did. I adored every last bit of this story 'here be sexist vampires' is escape from reality perfection and it doesn't harm that it delivered on all my five star must haves ... Here are my vampishly excited book thoughts.<br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>Samantha Parker has lived her vampire life under the control of her sire and captor, resigned to the fact that she is at the bottom of the pile and food chain when it comes to her importance as a vampire nothing comes as more of a shock when she is approached by a vampire of royal like status to request she joins a legion of the highest regard, it looks like this sassy talented Sventé vampire has just found her ticket to freedom. Sam approaches her new position with confidence and new found excitement but that soon has a damper put on it in the form of her new co-worker, heir to the Kingdom commander Jared Micheals, Jared doesn't appreciate having a female taking his side as his new colleague especially a vampire of such notably little status, Jared is more than happy to do things his way or no way. But Sam is not a vampire who is taking no for an answer and as her talents emerge so does a connection between this couple that can only be described as electric, but there are obstacles that stand in the way of this duo expressing how they really feel, can two people from different ways of life really make it the whole way to true love?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381396346i/4803092._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>Undoubtedly I have to start my gushing thoughts by talking about Sam the books heroine. Sam is brash, courageous, fearless and gorgeous I can't explain how much I loved this character her strength and beauty was as appealing as her humour and sarcastic nature; this lady is a real ball breaker and the author holds nothing back in delivering a character that is completing unforgettable. For every sassy heroine Suzanne Wright delivers in her books is an equally swoon worthy alpha, Jared ticked all my must have qualities for the perfect hero; out there manly, unsure of his pull towards his love for the heroine, gorgeous without measure, some arse hole chauvinist tendencies and most of all over protective 'that girl is mine' feelings. wrap all this up with some paranormal vampire activity and I had the perfect couple chemistry, I could not get enough of this duo. 'Here be sexist vampires' was utterly entertaining it had a range of qualities brought together with a fantastic writing style that I'm convinced most readers of this genre will be enthralled with. Drama, romance, chemistry and between the sheet action that can't be measured in the hotness scales. <br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>'Here be sexist' vampires takes the paranormal genre and gives it a hot comedy twist, the author is clearly a talented writer but you can also tell she enjoys what she does the love of her work leaks out of the pages and if I wasn't before I'm now a firm fan. This book is sexy hot, laugh out loud hilarious and Oscar worthy entertaining I can't recommend this book or the author enough. Don't wait any longer, go grab it readers. Enjoy ... Kisses.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15808297923879406615" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1727811213" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1727811213" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1727811213?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=girls-i-want-to-hang-out-with">girls-i-want-to-hang-out-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1727811213" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17391914844988693229">Oh my gosh, so much fun! And, I had a few doubts at first, but they were quickly thrown out the window as the baddest badass female heroine ever made me want her in my girl-tribe.<br/><br/>Sam (Samantha) is in the weakest of the three vampire races, but she has a special ability that is rarely seen and is therefore offered a job with the vampire king. Now, first I need to address the "special snowflake syndrome" that might go through your mind. Yes, she's special, but she isn't the most powerful vampire e</span>
  <span id="freeText17391914844988693229" style="display:none">Oh my gosh, so much fun! And, I had a few doubts at first, but they were quickly thrown out the window as the baddest badass female heroine ever made me want her in my girl-tribe.<br><br>Sam (Samantha) is in the weakest of the three vampire races, but she has a special ability that is rarely seen and is therefore offered a job with the vampire king. Now, first I need to address the "special snowflake syndrome" that might go through your mind. Yes, she's special, but she isn't the most powerful vampire ever, and she's not the fulfillment of some prophecy, or one of those girls who doesn't realize she's actually the most beautiful woman on Earth. Also, if she wasn't "special", would a book about a mundane vampire who does nothing be all that interesting? No, not really. Besides, once you meet Sam, you will allow a blizzard of special snowflakeness because she is so awesome.<br><br>Jared is a sexist pig who has three mistresses who live together in an apartment waiting for their opportunity to "serve" him. He's such an asshole that I really didn't want him to be her love interest for the first half of the book. But, I was underestimating Sam. She truly makes this guy work harder than the history of mankind to get on her good side. I appreciate a good ball-breaker when it is necessary. In Jared's case, it was very necessary. This guy needed a good old smack-down.<br><br>The two of them are forced to work together to prevent an attack on the Vamp King. They mix together about as well as broccoli and chocolate. Now, I know there is some freak out there who is saying, <i>"Oh, Jilly, I'm a foodie and chocolate covered broccoli is the latest thing."</i> First of all, shut up. We all eat food, therefore we are all "foodies". Secondly, how dare you blaspheme chocolate with vegetables? We already have people eating chocolate covered bacon, chili peppers, and bugs. When will the madness end?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471244927i/20014242._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>No. Just stop.</i><br><br>There is a ton of sexual tension between these two as well - much like the sexual tension between me and chocolate. (okay, I said it. It's out there now.) And, it is just as fun and delicious.<br><br>There is also a lot of magical fighting as the vampires are training for battle using their "gifts". Some of them can teleport, shoot poison, throw fire-balls, astro-project, and many other creative things. I loved the scenes where they were dueling each other, and then when they had the big battle. It made me really wish I could have a secret super-power, you know, other than the ability to make a pint of ice cream disappear. My other super-power immediately follows that one and is called shame.<br><br>The other part of the book that was fun for me, but could be difficult for some others was Sam's language. She is British and speaks in Cockney slang often. Although my husband is from the north, I still understood all of the slang, as he has used it at some point. But, I think most Americans would wonder what the hell she is saying half the time. Therefore, being the generous friend that I am, I have decided to provide you with a small glossary:<br><br><i>
  <b>He didn't tot around having a gander...</b>
</i> <br>I know what you are thinking - a tator tot eating goose. Of course. But, in this case, it means that he didn't wander around looking at everything. I know. A tator tot eating goose would be more fun. But, it wouldn't make as much sense. In this case.<br><br><i>
  <b>"..there's really no point in telling me porky pies.</b>
</i><br>Why would someone tell someone else about a meat pie? Did he make the meat pie? Does he need a food taster? No, and this is where it gets a little weird in England. They have this entire vocabulary called Cockney Rhyming Slang, and it's super bizarre yet they all know it. It works by substituting normal words or phrases with things that rhyme with them. So, it seems that at some point, there were some Cockneys with waaaay too much time on their hands. In the case of the above quote, porky pies means lies. Yes, my hubs uses this one. Along with many many others. If he wants to have a butchers at my dog and bone, I am not offended or afraid for my dog's life. It means he wants to look at my phone. I know. They are crazy and I married one.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471244927i/20014243._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471244927i/20014244._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>".. he said innocently like butter wouldn't melt in his mouth."</i>
</b><br>Who really wants to melt butter in their mouth anyway? We have microwaves for that. I've never considered melting it in my mouth and spitting it on my popcorn. Maybe Paula Deen would roll that way, but not me. But, for the Brits, this means that the person is playing it cool, nonchalant, aloof, coy. In other words they are so chill that their mouths are literally cold inside. Why is that a thing? I have no idea.<br><br>There are more, but I'm tired of typing, so if you have further questions, please direct them to me, Jilly, at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.google.com">www.google.com</a><br><br>And, read this book. It's fun.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17391914844988693229" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1949712041" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1949712041" />
    <a title="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews"><img alt="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1492999740p2/66199133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1949712041?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" href="/user/show/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews">Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=hot-jerks">hot-jerks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=reviews-of-the-year">reviews-of-the-year</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=favorite-heroine">favorite-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=guilty-pleasure">guilty-pleasure</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1949712041" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11698071827819299479">First... <b> I fucking love this title!</b> <br/> <br/>Now let me break it down for y'all: Vampire emperor, 3 unique breeds of vampires, threat of war on the balance, <b>and the FIRST gooddamn FEMALE COMMANDER of vampire ARMY!!! </b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443469835ra/16363689.gif' width='200' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/>Samantha aka <b>Sam</b> aka MANHH GURLL is one of the lowest ranking vampires but she don't take shit from anyone! And the fact she was so low and not as powerful honestly made her character 1000X better <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“God, I loved this woman: this very crazy, borderline-homicidal – on second thought, </i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText11698071827819299479" style="display:none">First... <b> I fucking love this title!</b> <br> <br>Now let me break it down for y'all: Vampire emperor, 3 unique breeds of vampires, threat of war on the balance, <b>and the FIRST gooddamn FEMALE COMMANDER of vampire ARMY!!! </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443469835ra/16363689.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Samantha aka <b>Sam</b> aka MANHH GURLL is one of the lowest ranking vampires but she don't take shit from anyone! And the fact she was so low and not as powerful honestly made her character 1000X better <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“God, I loved this woman: this very crazy, borderline-homicidal – on second thought, scrap the borderline – woman.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>She always had to work a little more than everyone ...cuz she was both the <b>weaker vampire AND a woman</b>. It was awesome watching her transform into the kickass, fabulous vampire heroine we know and love <i> *oh shit I got another girl crush now ??*</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1593096309ra/29707415.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>the love- interest <b> Jared</b> was totally a possessive asshole that Sam had to whip into shape in how he SUPPOSE to treat a woman <i>*hair flip*</i> <blockquote>
<b><i>“Jared’s lips were suddenly at my ear. “The only vampire who’ll be manhandling you tonight is me.”<br>“If I let you.”<br>“You get such satisfaction out of teasing me, don’t you?”<br>“I still maintain that you like it.”</i></b> </blockquote><br>They definitely had a fun-threatening banter that had me rooting for Sam the entire time. Also spoiler, Jared is absolutely the reason for the title <i>*figure it out*</i> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Whether she realized it yet or not, this betting stuff and the constant conflict between us was foreplay.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I also loved how the <b>secondary characters</b> were just as important and well developed as our main <br><br> oh my GOD I adored <b> FLETCHER</b> who was Sam's PA. He was such a loveable, engaging character and we get LGBT+ represent!! <i>*snaps*</i><br><br>If I had to describe it in a sentence, this was a great book with sexual tension, brutal training, finding a place within a sexist society, and....the fucking dialogue!<br><br> The author's british wit and humor came across each page with the character's slang <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> "He had to be blowing smoke up my arse" </i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br>But....my one complaint.... the one thing that fucking killed me in this book.... <br><br>In <b> what goddamn world </b> is it okay for <u>Sexy macho vampire</u> to be <b>GIGGLING</b> tHrOuGhOuT THIS ENTIRE fUcKiNg BOOK??!?!<br><br>I'm not kidding, <i>Everyone was just giggling</i> I did a search on the word and it popped up like 17x in one chapter! Like good god, let the man breathe <br><br>I'm reading about these gorgeous, tough 200-year-old vampires... just giggling all the time!<br>Basically the vampire warrior turned into silly schoolgirl. I don't think so. A chuckle-yes. Giggle-HELL NOO!!!! <br><br>But besides that weird annoying overused bit bid this was a great read, definitely recommend.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11698071827819299479" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17826184-here-be-sexist-vampires">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68070948-elena-c?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68070948-elena-c?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68070948-elena-c?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2096271857" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17716876634619847490">So, then, vampires are sexist. You know who else is sexist? <b>Suzanne Wright</b>.<br/><br/>But hey, Wright did her homework about sexism, worry not: so she knows it's, like, when men don't recognize women as their equals. Or something. That's why she came up with Sam, our resident kick-ass heroine, a "crazy bitch" with a foul mouth and an attitude who'll teach these misogynists what's what. Or something. <br/><br/>In Wright's vampire world, there are <b>two kinds of women</b>:<br/><br/>❶ <b>Sam</b>:<br/>● she doesn’t pay her appearance two shits (he</span>
  <span id="freeText17716876634619847490" style="display:none">So, then, vampires are sexist. You know who else is sexist? <b>Suzanne Wright</b>.<br /><br />But hey, Wright did her homework about sexism, worry not: so she knows it's, like, when men don't recognize women as their equals. Or something. That's why she came up with Sam, our resident kick-ass heroine, a "crazy bitch" with a foul mouth and an attitude who'll teach these misogynists what's what. Or something. <br /><br />In Wright's vampire world, there are <b>two kinds of women</b>:<br /><br />❶ <b>Sam</b>:<br />● she doesn’t pay her appearance two shits (her appearance being, we are constantly reassured, that of a Victoria’s Angel), so much so that she needs her gay sidekick’s counsel to buy clothes because, really, she can’t be bothered - she has asses to kick, sexist vampires to sass, some body shaming and slut shaming to throw around. Also, what else are gay men good for if not fixing your wardrobe? Duh;<br />● to Jared’s utter astonishment, she will occasionally have a Budweiser (as opposed to, say, a Cosmo or glass of rosé the rest of us womenfolk would drink);<br />● she can actually have a normal, friendly conversation with a male peer since, as she explains, “<i>he just finds it easy to talk to me because, unlike every other woman in The Hollow, I don’t mistake it for flirting and then try it on with him</i>.”<br />A very special lady indeed.<br /><br />❷ <b>Everyone else</b>. And let me tell you, if you were a male vampire, chances are you would be sexist too. Every single female vampire we meet is a sly, power-hungry brainless harpy who’ll resort to sex (what else?) to get her way and latch herself onto any male in a position of power. They don’t seem to be doing anything at all with their days but pout, purr, sensually lick their lips, strut around while looking luscious and inviting and wait for the booty call that will finally cement their social statuses.<br /><br />Having reassured her readers that yes, vampire society may be sexist, but rightfully so, Mrs. Wright then proceeds to illustrate why, exactly, Jared is such an asshole with women: they’ve been using him for sex, you see, sex and power. So, naturally, after a lifetime of abuse, he closed himself off emotionally and now only provides what little women ask of him. Thankfully Sam, being such a special special girl, sees right through his act and, after some more body shaming and slut shaming, she gets rid of her unworthy competition and wins Jared’s heart. <br /><br />What about the <b>smutty scenes</b>, you ask?<br />Mmm, well. Hot, they are hot. Sort of. I guess. But while reading them I had the weirdest feeling, like Wright’s only source of inspiration are the pirated porn videos from the early '90s you can watch on YouPorn - you know, those where a bulky dude violently grabs the woman by her hair and relentlessly pounds into her while shouting “YOU LIKE IT, HUH, TELL ME HOW MUCH YOU LIKE IT! TELL ME WHERE YOU LIKE IT, SAYTHATYOULIKEITBABYOHYES!BABYSAYITSAYITSAYIT!!!” in her face. <br /><br />SHUT UP, MAN.<br />And you, Suzanne Wright, get yourself a subscription to a decent porn film studio.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11472195705397331656">Re-read 11th - 12th February 2019<br/><br/>Re-read 9th July - 10th July 2018<br/><br/>Wow.<br/><br/>The question I asked myself several times while reading this book was 'why haven't I read this sooner?'<br/>I suppose in this case it's easy since neither the title nor the original cover appealed to me I'd continually skipped past it in fact it was only seeing my friends reviews come through that made me even look twice.<br/>The Phoenix Pack series by this author has been on my to-read list for years and once I've finished with 'Deep I</span>
  <span id="freeText11472195705397331656" style="display:none">Re-read 11th - 12th February 2019<br /><br />Re-read 9th July - 10th July 2018<br /><br />Wow.<br /><br />The question I asked myself several times while reading this book was 'why haven't I read this sooner?'<br />I suppose in this case it's easy since neither the title nor the original cover appealed to me I'd continually skipped past it in fact it was only seeing my friends reviews come through that made me even look twice.<br />The Phoenix Pack series by this author has been on my to-read list for years and once I've finished with 'Deep In Your Veins' I'm really going to have to get started on that.<br /><br />Anyway back to this book.<br /><br />Since I'm late to the party there's already so many excellent reviews so I'll keep mine brief. <br />I've spent years looking for a different, interesting vampire book and it was here all the time. Yet even without the different vampires and their amazing powers this book is worth reading for Sam and Sam alone. <br />Here is a strong intelligent female the kind that is missing from so many books. She's fabulous and a pleasure to read, there's no stupid here, no vacuous female that turns to idiot mode half way through making you wonder how she even dresses herself on a morning, Sam is brilliant.<br />She starts strong and stays strong and the rest of the book is just as good, the only slight problem I had was Jared at times but there's a story there which I'm sure will come out explaining his behaviour at times.<br /><br />This was so good and so enjoyable I'm giving 5* which is a rating I don't often give and it's straight on to 'The Bite That Binds' for me now.</span>

        <a title="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" href="/user/show/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed">Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17826184-here-be-sexist-vampires">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=2016">2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=challenge-2016">challenge-2016</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1392286214" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3699213585795138715">Listen book, I know it's not your fault that your author doesn't know what a thesaurus is, but I can't give you 5 stars when you use the word <u>giggle</u> in such excess that I want to cauterize the word out of you. Why would any author use <i>giggle</i>, fucking <b>giggle</b> to describe how all the men laugh, at all times. There are no guffaws, deep belly laughs, chuckles, or chortles to be had in this book. You get a laugh or snicker here or there, but fuck the word giggle. Now that that's off my back, to the ac</span>
  <span id="freeText3699213585795138715" style="display:none">Listen book, I know it's not your fault that your author doesn't know what a thesaurus is, but I can't give you 5 stars when you use the word <u>giggle</u> in such excess that I want to cauterize the word out of you. Why would any author use <i>giggle</i>, fucking <b>giggle</b> to describe how all the men laugh, at all times. There are no guffaws, deep belly laughs, chuckles, or chortles to be had in this book. You get a laugh or snicker here or there, but fuck the word giggle. Now that that's off my back, to the actual content...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455223467i/18075969.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book was similar-ish to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1130935125?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Chosen</a>, if it was about vampires and not as slice and dicing awesome. Sam is a Svente vampire with a colossally badass gift that allows her to control people's energies and the elements' energies. She's an avatar! And I thought Aang was the last air bender. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455223467i/18075970._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>She's described as a crazy and homicidal bitch. I agree with this statement and appreciate her for it. She's not a bitch in the way of you need to shank her, more like she's got a snappy mouth on her. She's in an all guy's world where there are zero female soldier vampires or Svente vampires. She's ticking off a lot of "hell no" boxes for people and getting tons of flack for her vamp type and being a chick. She responds with violence. I like it. It's always good to slap sense into men, and if that doesn't work, beat some more. Her job with the legion is to teach the recruits how to more adeptly control their gifts/energies. All the men of course think they don't need help from a female, so she beats them, obviously. <br><br>Jared is kind of like Mr. Cayan Pepper, except he puts out. ::side eye to Cayan::. He desperately wants to put out actually, but Sam isn't into being another one of his consorts, which she describes as prostitutes that do it for free. They're his mistresses I guess you could say and since he's not offering anything but that, she continuously declines him, even if they about set each other on fire with all the sexual tension. Jared is a commander and not at all happy to be working with a female Svente, especially one that can totally beat his ass in a fight. He's super misogynist, chauvinistic, and a right bastard to Sam for 90% of the book. Possibly more. All throughout the book she proves to him again and again that she's awesome and he should watch out for a kick to the nuts if he makes another snide comment. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455223467i/18075971._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So that's the book. Sam teaching the recruits, fending off the sexual attraction to Jared, showing the menfolk that she's more powerful than they are, and waiting to battle. The plot isn't huge, it's enough for this book. I enjoyed the sense of humor in the book and reading about a new vampire myos. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3699213585795138715" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer8500976054046128505">I've read the Phoenix pack series by this author, and since I loved those books, I thought I would give this one a try. Holy shit this book was good. I want to be her when I grow up ;)<br><br>Jared...he was one hell of a hot badass, alpha asshole. I love that asshole. So when I grow up to be Sam, I want a Jared for myself !!!<br><br>I thought all books were about different characters, but it turns out that the first three books are about Sam and Jared and only the fourth one is about a different couple. That's just fine by me, because the more we get about Sam and Jared the better. She totally kicked his asshole ass !!<br><br>There are a lot of reviews out here, that explain what this book is about. I'm not going to, because I find it very difficult to explain paranormal books. But if you love vampires, feisty strong funny females, hot alpha men, and some delicious steam, then I suggest you read this one :)<br><br>5 stars from me !!<br><br><a href="http://s172.photobucket.com/user/Wendy_Ciliacus/media/tumblr_lpfibkrKnq1qk6tevo1_500_zpsjucvnc46.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1239017131" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1239017131" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1239017131?book_show_action=true">Dec 20, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=girl-power">girl-power</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-leading-lady">best-leading-lady</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=alpha-male-love">alpha-male-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=love-this-author">love-this-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=2018-favorite">2018-favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=high-steam-alert">high-steam-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=rich-hottie">rich-hottie</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1239017131" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16835464726726956527"><blockquote>
  <b>“The only vampire who’ll be manhandling you tonight is me.”</b>
</blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1546489932i/26851419._SX540_.jpg' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Here be Sexiest Vampires</b> is the first book in the Deep In Your Veins Series and to say I am late for the party is the understatement of the century. In true Wright fashion, this paranormal romance is a delicious delight full of action, suspense, and passionate vampire love. Sam Parker is a Sventé vampire who has been held captive by her maker. When The Grand High Master offers her the opportunity of a lifetime, she jumps at the chanc</span>
  <span id="freeText16835464726726956527" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>“The only vampire who’ll be manhandling you tonight is me.”</b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1546489932i/26851419._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Here be Sexiest Vampires</b> is the first book in the Deep In Your Veins Series and to say I am late for the party is the understatement of the century. In true Wright fashion, this paranormal romance is a delicious delight full of action, suspense, and passionate vampire love. Sam Parker is a Sventé vampire who has been held captive by her maker. When The Grand High Master offers her the opportunity of a lifetime, she jumps at the chance. Sam has been escorted to his home where she has been invited to try out for his royal guard. Jared, a Pagori commander, wants nothing to do with Sam and certainly doesn't want her serving in the guard. But when Sam establishes herself as a force to be reckoned with Jared's disdain turns to complete adoration. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466701540i/19510149._SX540_.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>"Sam. I’m going to fuck you hard and fast until you come so hard you scream."</b>
</blockquote> Told in multiple POV, <b>Here Be Sexiest Vampires</b> is a paranormal blockbuster with non-stop action, witty banter, complex characters, and a twisted plot. The connection between Jared and Sam runs hot and cold as both learn to put their trust in the other. The paranormal world created by Ms. Wright, is quite magical with multiple characters, supernatural powers, seduction, and smoking hot passion. <blockquote>
  <b>"Even then, even that very first day, I couldn't shake that feeling that you were mine."</b>
</blockquote> Overall, <b>Here be Sexiest Vampires</b> is an absolute must read to paranormal romance fans who enjoy an over protective alpha male and a spunky heroine who gives as good as she gets! I am truly thrilled to have discovered this series and I look forward to reading them all! <br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:<br><a href="https://craziesrusbookblog.wordpress.com//" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483747845i/21645810.jpg" width="320" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450764696i/17467413.jpg" width="" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><a href="https://twitter.com/CraziesRus" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450633462i/17450183.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/craziesrus/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450763751i/17467332.jpg" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Crazies-R-Us-Book-Blog-171506803016307/timeline/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450633462i/17450182.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/110273454171852792166/posts" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451963666i/17626541.png" width="55" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450764696i/17467413.jpg" width="" height="30" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2718616127" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4425936237074701199"><strong>Suzanne Wright and Vampires! Need I say more?</strong><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1587054401ra/29303092.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Badass Vampire Chick meets sexist Vampire! There are three races of Vampires and two of them are elite while one is looked at as lower class. Samantha is one of the Svente vampires that are generally looked down upon, but her vampire gift is one that is rare and usually only ever seen in Pagori Vampires which are the highest class. <br/><br/>Sam is invited to the island by the High Grand Master Vampire to test to be in one of his security squads and she finds o</span>
  <span id="freeText4425936237074701199" style="display:none"><strong>Suzanne Wright and Vampires! Need I say more?</strong><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1587054401ra/29303092.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Badass Vampire Chick meets sexist Vampire! There are three races of Vampires and two of them are elite while one is looked at as lower class. Samantha is one of the Svente vampires that are generally looked down upon, but her vampire gift is one that is rare and usually only ever seen in Pagori Vampires which are the highest class. <br><br>Sam is invited to the island by the High Grand Master Vampire to test to be in one of his security squads and she finds out that not only is she the first Svente Vampire to try out, but also the first woman. Though she will do almost anything to get away from her brutal sire. <br><br>The test is three trials and the main commander that is rating the participants is heir to the High Grand Masters throne, Jared Michaels. He already told her she should just walk away before she embarrasses herself.<br>Sam is attracted to Jarred from the start, and he is attracted to her. Though he already has three consorts, he wouldn’t mind adding her as an additional one. Of course Sam refuses to be a consort and Jared just can’t understand why since he is a sexist pig. <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> Just then, Antonio entered with his two guards, Pit Bulls. Behind them were Sebastian and a strange, tall Keja with long white-grey hair and a matching long beard. That’s Luther, Jared informed me. He’s Antonio’s Advisor. Someone should tell him that he’s not living in the film Lord of the Rings. Jared coughed to hide his chuckle.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>The story is Sam being completely badass and proving she is not only his equal, but so much better until he finally sees things clearly. She never backs down, which is what I really like. Plus I do like it when misogynistic jerks finally figure it out and start behaving like they have a clue.<br><br><a href="https://www.ilikebooksbest.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a>|<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/wennel" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a>|<a href="https://www.facebook.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>|<a href="https://www.instagram.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a>|<a href="https://www.twitter.com/wendysu020202" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>|<a href="https://www.bookbub.com/profile/1895823057" rel="nofollow noopener">BookBub</a></span>

She can feed on the energy surrounding her, absorb it and control it. She can also take gifts from other vampires </span>
  <span id="freeText15028811298047329785" style="display:none"><b>4 Sexist Stars</b><br><br><br>It's official, Suzanne Wright writes the absolute best female leads! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/545171.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Sam is smart, mouthy, strong, mouthy, level-headed, did I mention she is mouthy? Loved her!!<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381800320ra/5313141.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Sam is a Svente vampire. These vampires are more human like than the Pagoris (known for their super strength) and Kejas (known for their hypnotic beauty). All vampires have gifts. Sam's gift is she is a Feeder. She can feed on the energy surrounding her, absorb it and control it. She can also take gifts from other vampires temporarily. This is where she meets Commander Jared Michaels. <br><br><br><b>

He sees it as wanting to keep her safe as the thought of losing her is too much for him. Can they find a middle ground?<br><br><br><b>
