<div id="review_578515306" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578515306" />
    <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet"><img alt="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1387046887p2/13567836.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/578515306?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet">Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=pn-vampires">pn-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=pn-romance">pn-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=read-more-than-once">read-more-than-once</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=possessive-controlling-men">possessive-controlling-men</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=sexy-alpha-male">sexy-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer578515306" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1054870215240979517"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Is There Something Wrong With Me?*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 27.10.19</u>
</b><br/>I've changed, that's for sure. While I love Jared, I also found him - this time around - bratty, annoying, childish and frankly...weak. As for Sam - this time around - I find a bit too strong headed. While I understand her reasons, it's just, yeah, too much. Also, something I've noticed why reading paranormal/fantasy lately, it that the women in them are just so <i>powerful</i>, <i>unique</i> and <i>perfect</i> and so forth... and <b>it's st</b></span>
  <span id="freeText1054870215240979517" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Is There Something Wrong With Me?*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 27.10.19</u>
</b><br>I've changed, that's for sure. While I love Jared, I also found him - this time around - bratty, annoying, childish and frankly...weak. As for Sam - this time around - I find a bit too strong headed. While I understand her reasons, it's just, yeah, too much. Also, something I've noticed why reading paranormal/fantasy lately, it that the women in them are just so <i>powerful</i>, <i>unique</i> and <i>perfect</i> and so forth... and <b>it's starting to get a bit annoying</b>, specially in all my re-reads. I get that women aren't weak and all that, but when it's over the top? It becomes too much for me. This happened with other books too, like my one of my favorite series <b>
  <i>The Fae Chronicles</i>
</b>, which I stopped reading. <br><br>But <b>
  <i>Suzanne Wright</i>
</b> did get it right with Taryn in <b>
  <i>Feral Sins</i>
</b>, and other authors has gotten it right (in my opinion) as well like Cat in <b>
  <i>Night Huntress</i>
</b> by <b>
  <i>Jeaniene Frost</i>
</b>, Kate in <b>
  <i>Kate Daniel</i>
</b> by <b>
  <i>Ilona Andrews</i>
</b>. But Sam in this one? It's a bit over the top for me. Specially in the first book in the series. She's just too powerful, too great, too good, too fantastic..... and of course everyone loves her or wants her. And making the one who's supposed to be so powerful look quite weak. And <b>I'm a huge fan of POWERFUL alpha males</b>, and getting his ass handed to him by this all powerful woman who's just so powerful, makes me <i>not</i> think of him as powerful at all. Is that the meaning? <br><br>Overall, I don't regret re-reading it, I don't, the story is still interesting, with interesting characters, but it's not my favorite of the author (that will always and forever be Feral Sins). I don't get why every author these days makes all their main female character so damn powerful that <b>it makes it too unrealistic even in a fantasy world (for me)</b>. I just want my men all powerful in my BOOKS (not in real world, guys), but in the books I read, I want the main male to be the one who everyone fears and who has no equal and so forth. Perhaps that makes me petty or not supporting of female characters, but that just how I want it in the BOOKS I read. <br><br>Like Kate Daniels is the perfect female character; she's incredible powerful, <b>even more powerful than Curran, but it's written <i>right</i> in a way that doesn't make Curran look weak in order to make her look powerful, or more powerful</b>. Also I have to say that I struggled a bit with the <i>giggling</i> parts. It's just something I picture little girls doing, not grown male vampires or the Grand High Master... (<b>
  <i>“Oh God. Another shudder began to crest. I tried holding it back but a tremor still ventured through me. Jared felt it and giggled.”</i>
</b>)<br><br><b><u>The Main Characters</u>:</b><br>→ <b>Sam</b> (23, turned vampire at 20), a Sventé vampire. She's a Feeder: feeds on the energy around you; absorb it and control it. Can shape the energy into lots of different weapons. Bolts, beams, balls, whip. Feeding on energy means that you can tap into the natural energies: the classical elements; air, water, fire and earth. Feeders are very rare. Most go crazy and die after a few years because all the energy overwhelms them. The gift has only ever run through Pagori bloodlines before Sam, which means that not only are she the first female Feeder, she's the first Sventé Feeder. Sam has tremendous control. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Later, after Sam kills her Sire to protect Antionio, Antonio gives Sam a new gift: the gift of Merger: she can merge with other people/animals. This is also a gift that runs in the Pagori lines. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>→ Commander <b>Jared Michaels</b> (18 years as a vampire, 24 years as a human), a Pagori Master vampire. His natural gift is electrokinesis, but Antonio has the power to pass on gifts. Twice he singled Jared out to receive two others as rewards: teleportion and telepathy (communication using his mind but cannot read thoughts). Jared is Antonio's Hair. Out of hundreds, he made Jared his Heir six years ago. He and Sam will be commanding the new squad of ten that replaced the old squad of the Grand High Master, that was recently annihilated.<br><br><b><u>Vampire breeds</u>:</b><br><i>I put this in a spoiler tag as the text is long.</i><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[→ <b>Pagori</b>:<br>They are naturally irritable and easily become aggressive, and has hulk-like strength and speed. Their irises flashes red/They a red tint to their irises. When irises glow they are either pissed, horny or thirsty.<br>→ <b>Keja</b>:<br>Recognizable by the slight tint of amber in their irises. That amber would glow whenever he/she was angry, thirsty or horny. They have fangs. All Keja vampires had hypnotic beauty and females were often called Enchantresses. <br>→ <b>Sventé</b>:<br>Are considered lower class by the other vampire breeds because they are considered ‘too tame’. Though they are stronger and faster than any human, they lack the super-super-super strength, speed (Pagori) and hypnotic beauty (Kejas) that the other two breeds has. But their bloodlust isn’t overpowering which means that they can walk amongst humans without becoming overwhelmed and tempted to cling to someone’s artery. Typically Sventé gifts were only ever defensive rather than offensive. Or ‘boring’, as most complained. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b><u>The recruits</u>:</b><br><i>I put this in a spoiler tag as the list is long.</i><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[→ <b>Reuben</b>, a Pagori vampire. Turned at the age of thirty and had been a vampire for sixty years. Aptitude tests showed him to not be the brightest bulb, but he certainly made up for it in the physical department; he was by far the strongest and was built like a body builder. His gift was power augmentation, meaning that he could weaken or strengthen the gift of another. <br>→ <b>Stuart</b>, a Pagori vampire, who had been eighteen when Turned over thirty years ago. He was a Shredder: his gift allowed him to disband until he was nothing but molecules and then reform again at will. <br>→ <b>Chico</b>, the thorn-exhaling Keja vampire (from Sam's tryout). Was little on the podgy side he was physically just as able as the others, and was the smartest of the squad. Apparently the poison in the thorns caused the victim to instantly lose consciousness for a period of up to five hours.<br>→ <b>Robert ‘Butch’ Richardson</b>, a Pagori vampire (from Sam's tryout). A Negator: he could completely cancel out any power aimed at him.<br>→ <b>Max ‘Slap-head’</b>, a Pagori vampire (from Sam's tryout). At the age of twenty-six he had been Turned and had been a vampire for just over twenty years. He had the power to cause temporary sensory paralysis, which meant his opponent was rendered blind, deaf and mute. As such, he was shooting his superhuman breath blindly – literally. His weakness, however, was in his agility.<br>→ <b>David</b>, a Keja vampire and the youngest of the squad; Turned at seventeen and had only been a vampire for three years (same vampire life-span as Sam). He didn’t have much to boast off with regards to strength and speed, but he had an amazing power to attack an opponent with: a psionic boom, something which caused extreme pressure on the skull and completely overwhelmed the brain, leading to either a temporary coma or death depending on the strength of the blast.<br>→ <b>Damien</b>, a Pagori vampire only a year older in vampire years than David and Sam, and was Turned when twenty-four. Apparently is the fastest of the squad and excellent at one-to-one combat. Damien’s gift was Astral Projection, but apparently his consciousness wasn’t able to travel far from his body.<br>→ <b>Edward ‘Salem’</b>, a Pagori vampire. Turned at the age of thirty-six just over forty-eight years ago. His gift enabled him to emit an invisible blast of psychic energy that could render an opponent completely unconscious. Basically, he had a psychic punch.<br>→ <b>Harvey</b>, a Pagori vampire. He was just nineteen when Turned just under twelve years ago. Harvey was telekinetic; which meant that he would be able to move something or someone without physically touching it.<br>→ <b> Dennis ‘Denny’</b>, a Pagori vampire. A vampire for over seventy years, he had been twenty when Turned. His athletic physique didn’t do his strength and speed justice. He also had the best reflexes of all the recruits. He has the gift of animal mimicry: animal-like abilities. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b><u>Other Characters</u>:</b><br><i>I put this in a spoiler tag as the list is long.</i><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[→ <b>Victor</b>, Sam's Sire, who was low, low, low, low down in the hierarchy , which was why he persistently duelled for more territory and had used Sam for the past three years (since he turned her) to help with his pursuit of it. Sam has also been Vince’s consort against her will for the past three years. Sam was the Chief Assassin for Victor and went on a hell of a lot of assignments – some on her own, some with a squad of eight. She always got her target, and she always brought all eight back. Victor’s a master at manipulation: he can manipulate your emotions. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sam kills him protecting Antonio at 30% into the book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br>→ <b>Sebastian</b>, who works directly for the Grand High Master; the vampire of all vampires. Sebastian's a Tracker, who's job is to hunt and seize felons as directed by their Grand High Master. However, his main role for the past two weeks has been to scout in search of any suitable candidates for His Grandness replacements for an exterminated squad in his private army, his legion.<br>→ <b>Antonio</b>, the Grand High Master and a Keja vampire. <b>Nero</b> and <b>Achilles</b>, Antonio's Pit Bull dogs. Antonio is a Bestower: he can impart power to a vampire, not energy, that is different. Power. It can only be done at his control, but he cannot control what reaction the power has to your own innate concentration of power. In other words, he do not know what gift you will then develop, but it will not be his own.<br>→ <b>Fletcher ‘Fletch’</b>, a Keja vampire and an Empath (can sense the emotions of people near to them), who has been Jared’s assistant for the past three years, and now he is also Sam's. A fellow Brit, too (Sam's British). <b>Norm</b>, his boyfriend, an office guard.<br>→ Commander <b>Evan Michaels</b>, Jared’s brother; twins. Both got Turned into vamps at the same time.<br>→ <b>Green</b>, a Pagori vampire.<br>→ Commander <b>Will Norton</b>, a Pagori vampire<br>→ Commander <b>Lou Sherman</b>, a Keja vampire.<br>→ Commander <b>Dawson</b>, a Pagori vampire.<br>→ Commander <b>Marsh</b>, a vampire.<br>→ Commander <b>Donnie Rodney</b>, a vampire.<br>→ Commander <b>McGowan</b>, a Pagori vampire. <br>→ Commander <b>Baker</b>, a Pagori vampire. Has a hyena laugh.<br>→ Commander <b>Rowan</b>, a Pagori vampire. A whistler.<br>→ Commander <b>White</b>, a vampire.<br>→ <b>Joy</b>, a Keja vampire and a favorite consort of Jared. She has the gift of Physical Imitation: she can morphe into someone else.<br>→ <b>Daniela</b> and <b>Tammy</b>, the other two consorts of Jared. Both Keja vampires too. The consorts share a apartment together<br>→ <b>Luther</b>, Antonio’s Advisor. A Keja vampire who had long white-grey hair and a matching long beard. He has the gift of precognition. Part of Luther’s gift is that he can allow another person to have a vision of their own merely through touch. He would not see your vision, only you would.<br>→ <b>Bennington</b>, the Sventé High Master. British like Sam, had quite a reputation for collecting gifted vampires. Sam has met him a few times and has tried to buy her from Victor, but even though Victor barely had any money he refused to hand her over for any price. Bennington's gift is to measure the power voltage coming from other vampires. Using this gift, he has compensated for his own ill defense by selecting extremely gifted vampires to build himself a team of bodyguards. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Jared kills him in battle at the end of the book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b> Rupert Connelly</b>, a High Master Keja vampire over the entire Caribbean and other places like Hawaii and Brazil. He’s about three centuries old and he’s got a rod stuck up his ass (Jared's opinion), but he’s devoted to Antonio.<br>→ <b>Bran</b>, a High Master Keja vampire over Japan, China, and Africa among other places. He’s always been a close friend of Antonio’s, they have the same Sire. He’s an Ecological Empath; he has a psychic sensitivity to his surrounding environment. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>Alora</b>, Bran’s Consort, who is the girl from Evan's vision from Luther. Her gift: can communicate with and charm animals. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b>Kaiser</b>, a High Master Pagori vampire over Germany, Russia, Sweden, Finland and other places round those parts. Loyal to Antonio. His gift: can petrify any plant, animal or even human – totally turning them to stone. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Paranormal Romance (M/F).<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book One. <br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Not really. Max is interested in Sam, but we all know Jared's the one for her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[For now. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Jared Michaels, I think. He's hot in bed.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Sure, I guess.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - Unsure now...<br><b>New Rating</b> - 3 stars.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 14.08.2016</u>
</b><br>Still awesome. I love Sam and Jared. And I <i>really</i> love it when Jared called Sam <i>baby</i>. I don't know why, but it just gets me...<br><b>Rating</b> - 4 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

</blockquote><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397413i/766850.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>And why did the idea of her in danger make me feel ill inside? For the same reason that the idea of her in danger scared the crap out of me: I loved the crazy bitch.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397413ra/766851.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>I love that Sam is a super strong female character and holds her own when everything is against her. I applaud you Suzanne!<i></i></i></span>

<div id="review_266944054" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/266944054" />
    <a title="Nicola" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4092821-nicola"><img alt="Nicola" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/266944054?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nicola" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nicola" href="/user/show/4092821-nicola">Nicola</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer266944054" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9208821164441433795">I enjoyed this book - nice storyline, great characters (especially Sam!) and full of humour. <br/><br/>However, I will say that the experience was marred a little bit by a few things.<br/><br/>There were a few little mistakes scattered throughout the book which didn't bother me overmuch, but the repeated use of 'seen' instead of 'seeing' (as in, 'seen as' instead of 'seeing as' or 'seen that' instead of 'seeing that so and so') was a bit distracting. <br/><br/>I also wished that the characters weren't constantly described as</span>
  <span id="freeText9208821164441433795" style="display:none">I enjoyed this book - nice storyline, great characters (especially Sam!) and full of humour. <br /><br />However, I will say that the experience was marred a little bit by a few things.<br /><br />There were a few little mistakes scattered throughout the book which didn't bother me overmuch, but the repeated use of 'seen' instead of 'seeing' (as in, 'seen as' instead of 'seeing as' or 'seen that' instead of 'seeing that so and so') was a bit distracting. <br /><br />I also wished that the characters weren't constantly described as giggling. Fair enough once or twice, but reading about the gorgeous, tough manly vampires giggling all the time kind of wrecked the image for me - a laugh, yes; a giggle, no. It seemed as though the characters mainly alternated between giggling or glaring, which I thought was used out of context a few times too. I associate glaring with anger or annoyance, but they were described as glaring at each other with a different kind of emotion a couple of times. <br /><br />A little more polishing and this book would be 4 stars for me, but on the whole a nice funny read. I'll definitely be reading any future books that come out. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9208821164441433795" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15329568829118947066">When Sam Parker was turned into a vampire, she did not realize her life would take a dramatic turn. As a consort/assassin for the last three years for her vile maker, Sam just tries to get by on a daily basis looking for an out. That out comes in the form of a mind changing offer, try out for the Grand High Masters Vampire Army. It is a rare offer especially for a woman, but Sam's gifts are unprecedented and would be a huge asset to the Army.<br/><br/>Of course when she meets Commander and heir to the Gra</span>
  <span id="freeText15329568829118947066" style="display:none">When Sam Parker was turned into a vampire, she did not realize her life would take a dramatic turn. As a consort/assassin for the last three years for her vile maker, Sam just tries to get by on a daily basis looking for an out. That out comes in the form of a mind changing offer, try out for the Grand High Masters Vampire Army. It is a rare offer especially for a woman, but Sam's gifts are unprecedented and would be a huge asset to the Army.<br /><br />Of course when she meets Commander and heir to the Grand Master, Jarod, he makes his intent clear she is perfectly suited as a..consort and the sooner she comes to his bed the quicker she can go back to her life. Sam though has other ideas, including whipping his ass for his sexist behavior. The challenge is set and when Jarod is told Sam will not be his trainee rather his co-worker, all bets are off the temperamental vixen has Jarod determined to make her is, but she won't settle to be treated as a piece of meat in his harem.<br /><br />Absolutely one of the funnest vampire stories I have read in a long time, Sam is a kick in the pants and tough to boot. She completely keeps Jarod off guard and he struggles, boy does he struggle with his arrogant demeanor. Definitely reread worthy.</span>

<div id="review_566813129" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/566813129" />
    <a title="Shera (Book Whispers)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3167178-shera-book-whispers"><img alt="Shera (Book Whispers)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1446841556p2/3167178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/566813129?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shera (Book Whispers)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shera (Book Whispers)" href="/user/show/3167178-shera-book-whispers">Shera (Book Whispers)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3167178-shera-book-whispers?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3167178-shera-book-whispers?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3167178-shera-book-whispers?shelf=vampire">vampire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3167178-shera-book-whispers?shelf=2012">2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer566813129" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13578385173949996712">Giggling. It is a word I now cringe to see on the page. Everybody giggles in this book. Laughing and chuckling do not exist. Every time a strong male character, or even the lead herself, started giggling I was completely pulled out of the book. In real life giggling is annoying, I think on the page it's only made more annoying. Don't even get me started on some of the other grammatical errors. <br/><br/>Yes, this book made me laugh. No, the plot was not engaging. The male lead, Jake, was horrible. He is a</span>
  <span id="freeText13578385173949996712" style="display:none">Giggling. It is a word I now cringe to see on the page. Everybody giggles in this book. Laughing and chuckling do not exist. Every time a strong male character, or even the lead herself, started giggling I was completely pulled out of the book. In real life giggling is annoying, I think on the page it's only made more annoying. Don't even get me started on some of the other grammatical errors. <br /><br />Yes, this book made me laugh. No, the plot was not engaging. The male lead, Jake, was horrible. He is a sexist prick and up to the point that I read to he doesn't get over it. The strong female lead justifies his action. The excuse that he's a man in power and is just enjoying the perks of those powers does not cut it. He treats his three concubines horribly! He doesn't treat them like humans, but possessions. Even after he develops and admits his feelings for Sam he's still sexist. Jake never truly makes the revelation that the way he acts towards woman is wrong, even after he gets his HEA with Sam. <br /><br />Sam is a strong female and the character that is being built does not fit the stupidity that leaps out and slaps the readers. She doesn't want to be a possession anymore, but she lusts after Jake immediately even after she realizes he’s a sexist jerk. My understanding is that there love makes her accept Jake's over bearing personality, possessiveness, and all that annoying stuff. But I didn't feel it. <br /><br />The book is rough, and I'm beyond disappointed by all the positive reviews. Even if the story was brilliant, the writing would have pulled it down. Here Be Sexist Vampires tries too hard. The few laughs were great, but the story was frustrating. <br /><br /><b>Sexual Content:</b> The majority of the book has no sex scenes. There’s plenty of sexual humor abound. A few sites have this labeled under erotica, to me it reads like a PNR. The most mild erotica I have ever read. <br /><br /><b>1/5- I couldn't finish it or wish I hadn't </b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Originally reviewed at <a href="http://www.shera-bookwhispers.blogspot.com/2013/06/review-here-be-sexist-vampires.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Book Whispers</a>.</i>
</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5201842166522934315">A few weeks ago I was spoiling a book… I was having very much fun… my friend Iva a little less! *wink*<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427088i/853773.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So she said she’ll forgive my bad behaviour if I read this book.<br/><br/>Since I really want her forgiveness I’ve read it and … <b>SHE WAS RIGHT!!!<br/><br/>This book is really, really good!!!</b> <br/><br/>I thought that this would be a usual vampire book, but it was not!<br/><br/>Here the vampires are like super-heroes in Marvel’s comics.<br/><br/>Sam, the heroine, is awesome! She’s strong, she’s sassy, she’s smart and she’s hilarious! <br/><br/><i> “God, give </i></span>
  <span id="freeText5201842166522934315" style="display:none">A few weeks ago I was spoiling a book… I was having very much fun… my friend Iva a little less! *wink*<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427088i/853773.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So she said she’ll forgive my bad behaviour if I read this book.<br><br>Since I really want her forgiveness I’ve read it and … <b>SHE WAS RIGHT!!!<br><br>This book is really, really good!!!</b> <br><br>I thought that this would be a usual vampire book, but it was not!<br><br>Here the vampires are like super-heroes in Marvel’s comics.<br><br>Sam, the heroine, is awesome! She’s strong, she’s sassy, she’s smart and she’s hilarious! <br><br><i> “God, give me strength,” I begged as I looked upwards. “I’m bored with Question Time now, Dickson.”<br>“It’s Dawson.”<br>“I know.”</i><br><br>As soon as she appeared and confronted Jared, the hero, I loved her! She’s so confident and she wouldn’t allow anyone to stomp on her for any reason! Obviously, having a job as the firs woman Commander, she has to fight and prove to everybody that she’s capable and she does a great job! She’s devious and she manages to become a fantastic commander! Great!!!<br>We know right from the start that she’s attracted to Jared. She doesn’t negate it, but she fights it for all the good reasons: she doesn’t want to be his possession. She want to be respected. <br><br>Jared is a spoilt boy. He’s the Heir and he wallows in his role. <br><br><i>“Tell me you’re not here hoping to try for a place in the legion.” When I didn’t say anything he laughed. “Let me give you some advice: run along home.”<br>“Why? Because I’m a girl?”<br>“Yes.”<br>What an arrogant little sod. I folded my arms across my chest and snorted. “Are you for real?”<br>“Listen, this isn’t a cheerleading squad. You don’t get points for being pretty. It’s some serious shit which is why a girl has never been accepted, and never will be. There’s no place for a female in the legion.”<br><br>---------------------------------------------<br><br>I had my ass kicked. I had my ass kicked by a Sventé vampire. I had my ass kicked by a woman. The guys would never let me live this down. </i><br><br>Every female is at his feet and he doesn’t understand why Sam is not among them. She confuses him and challenges him. Obviously, that is what make him notice her. His attraction grows and grows until it just snaps. But still he doesn’t get that Sam is not a simple female: she’s his equal, but he doesn’t want to acknowledge it. So he pursues her, he teases her, he challenges her authority as Commander. But Sam is strong: fighting fair she just confuses him more. Bit by bit Sam makes him understand her and it happens slowly until Jared is so deep in love with her that when he realizes it he’s shocked and elated in the same time! <br><br><br>The dialogue, the secondary characters, the action, the fun moments, the heat and the sex are great! I love the tone of voice of the whole book. It was so fun and easy to read. Very refreshing!<br><br>So, if you want a vampire book with a different twist, you <b>must</b> read this one, you’ll not regret it! :D</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1374779660" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11491260040874745512">Actual Rating 2.5 stars<br/><br/>Meh, it's ok.<br/><br/>I found the main characters thoughts and feelings a bit contradictory and nonsensical, so it is not a surprise that the romance did not reach me at all. In addition, I didn't find the characters likable and the male protagonist put me off. <br/><br/>The aspects of the story revolving other characters were, at times, tiresome and overly detailed. Likewise, the relationship between some of the characters and their actions felt generally unrealistic. <br/><br/>The vampire side of th</span>
  <span id="freeText11491260040874745512" style="display:none">Actual Rating 2.5 stars<br /><br />Meh, it's ok.<br /><br />I found the main characters thoughts and feelings a bit contradictory and nonsensical, so it is not a surprise that the romance did not reach me at all. In addition, I didn't find the characters likable and the male protagonist put me off. <br /><br />The aspects of the story revolving other characters were, at times, tiresome and overly detailed. Likewise, the relationship between some of the characters and their actions felt generally unrealistic. <br /><br />The vampire side of things was feeble and lame. Very unsatisfying if you are a vampire lover like me, and you are looking for substance in the topic instead of having it as an add-on.<br /><br />Finally, even though the female protagonist complained about the sexism of the males in the book, she herself made some sexist comments, which bothers me greatly since it reflects a lack of actual understanding of what sexism really entails from the character/author who is championing equality here. Disappointing really, but I guess the effort is appreciated and much better than nothing. I would add that the background mentality in romantic/sexual relationships reflected here is not what I would personally consider consistent, reasonable and generally healthy. <br /><br />Overall, it feels cliché and even reminiscent at times of Twilight.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11491260040874745512" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Jamie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11971939-jamie"><img alt="Jamie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1450934094p2/11971939.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/466456454?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie" href="/user/show/11971939-jamie">Jamie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11971939-jamie?shelf=all-time-fav">all-time-fav</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer466456454" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4928629569900260649">WOW! I simply could not put this down.. the chemistry between Sam and Jared was scorching and their back and forth banter and ass kicking was all a bunch of serious foreplay... Sam is one super kick ass vamp and she takes no shit off of anyone.. she's beautiful, tough, but also with a soft sexy side. Jared is an extreamly hot dickhead who knows exactly how to push Sam's buttons.. and whoa.. does he press her buttons. Sam and Jared knew their feelings for each other for most of the book and didnt</span>
  <span id="freeText4928629569900260649" style="display:none">WOW! I simply could not put this down.. the chemistry between Sam and Jared was scorching and their back and forth banter and ass kicking was all a bunch of serious foreplay... Sam is one super kick ass vamp and she takes no shit off of anyone.. she's beautiful, tough, but also with a soft sexy side. Jared is an extreamly hot dickhead who knows exactly how to push Sam's buttons.. and whoa.. does he press her buttons. Sam and Jared knew their feelings for each other for most of the book and didnt deny it but they didnt really hook up till around 70% but it was worth the wait. The chemistry and lead up to it was awesome and I never felt like I was missing out on something. And once they did get together.. whew! Hottest Vamp sex ever. Lets just say that one of Jareds powers is that he can produce electricity through his fingertips.. and he used that power on Sam in some very VERY hot ways.. dang.. I dont even smoke and felt like I needed a cigarette after they hooked up. This is th 3rd book I've read by Suzanne Wright and each one has been beter than the last.. All of them have been amazing though. This one is my favorite. Its a MUST READ as far as I'm concerned. She is officailly on my MUST READ list. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3648030061111506864"> <b> 5 Great biting stars!!</b><br/><br/>I was in the mood for a vampire book (which is already weird since I’m not normally the biggest fan of PNR), and somehow this one stumbled on my sight. <br/>Well, it was a good thing that it did because this was just… awesome. <br/>Vampires totally got on my high ranking again! <br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431929ra/867022.gif' width='300' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So, basically Sam is a Sventé vampire, the less powerful of the three breeds of vampires, but she is unusual strong and gifted. <br/>So she is scouted to be a member of the High Master security team and anxious </span>
  <span id="freeText3648030061111506864" style="display:none"> <b> 5 Great biting stars!!</b><br><br>I was in the mood for a vampire book (which is already weird since I’m not normally the biggest fan of PNR), and somehow this one stumbled on my sight. <br>Well, it was a good thing that it did because this was just… awesome. <br>Vampires totally got on my high ranking again! <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431929ra/867022.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, basically Sam is a Sventé vampire, the less powerful of the three breeds of vampires, but she is unusual strong and gifted. <br>So she is scouted to be a member of the High Master security team and anxious to leave her horrible master she accepts. When she gets there she finds out that she have to deal with a lot of sexist and strong vampires that doesn’t believe in her capacities since she is not only a sventé but also a female. <br>Not that she cares… after all she is a badass bitch, so she puts everyone of them in their place. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431929ra/867023.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, everyone except Jared. One of the commanders and the Heir of the High Master. And he especially does not believe that she is capable of doing that job.<br>Forced to work together, things will heat: first their anger against each other, since they want to be in each other’s throat basically all the time. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431929i/867024.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But as she keeps proving her value and they get to know more about the other things start to change and anger gives place to other kind of feeling… and between a lot of action, drama and awesome things, hotness starts to come! And believe me, it is hot!!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431929i/867025.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, I read basically all the books from Suzanne Wright at this point, and boy, this woman as a real gift of creating the most sexy alpha-males and the most awesome badass heroines. I fell in love with her characters in every single book and this was no exception.<br>The book is just great, addicting and you just can’t stop reading it. Not to mention the steam (oh so steamy!) scenes. <br>If you’re into PNR (or even if you’re not!) you’re going to love this. Go read now, people ;) </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1336747372" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12085983418143968956"><b>Read 18th July 2015 - 5 Stars<br/>Reread 09th October - still 5 Stars. <br/><br/>This is the second time that Ms. Wright has got me out of my book funk. Ms. Wright is my go to author if I need a pick me up and I got this with Sam & Jared. <br/><br/>This isn’t your standard vampire series. It’s better. Much better, fucking brilliant. Sleep is really overrated if you ask me. Could. Not. Put. It. Down. 5 homicidal stars. <br/><br/>There are three different types of vampires. The Sventé; who are the most human and not as strong as th</b></span>
  <span id="freeText12085983418143968956" style="display:none"><b>Read 18th July 2015 - 5 Stars<br />Reread 09th October - still 5 Stars. <br /><br />This is the second time that Ms. Wright has got me out of my book funk. Ms. Wright is my go to author if I need a pick me up and I got this with Sam &amp; Jared. <br /><br />This isn’t your standard vampire series. It’s better. Much better, fucking brilliant. Sleep is really overrated if you ask me. Could. Not. Put. It. Down. 5 homicidal stars. <br /><br />There are three different types of vampires. The Sventé; who are the most human and not as strong as the other two breeds. The Keja: alluring but in the middle of the chain food system and the Pagori, strong, arrogant and full of themselves. Each vampire has a gift and it can be offensive or defensive.<br /><br />Sam Parker lives in London, she is a Brit and character wise she is my kind of girl. She is strong, blunt and hilarious to be around. She is oi this and bollocks that. She has been invited to try out for a position of the legion for the grand high master, Antonio. She has been used by her sire, Viktor. I don’t feel sorry for the bastard. She wants a better life and goes for it. Things that are in her way? A sexist vampire who is entirely too hot for his own good. <br /><br />Her first encounter with Jared Michaels doesn’t go that well. Yes, he is hot but he is also a chauvinistic, sexist, condescending prick. At the try outs she succeeds with flying colors and even puts pretty boy on his arse. <br /><br />Sam is a feeder and I love what she does with her powers-Jared is to be the next heir and lives a life of loneliness even with his three consorts. Man whore ahead! But he changes his ways more and even before Sam. <br /><br />Jared denies her a place within the legion but Antonio has the last word and makes her co-commander. Jared is pissed. Although they don’t like each other they want each other and they have serious chemistry. <br /><br />They slowly start to work out their differences. And develop a deep connection. I would go as far as to say that Jared is smitten with Sam. <br /><br />“God, I loved this woman: this very crazy, borderline-homicidal – on second thought, scrap the borderline – woman.”<br /><br />The banter and chemistry was great. <br /><br />“Jared’s lips were suddenly at my ear. “The only vampire who’ll be manhandling you tonight is me.”<br />“If I let you.”<br />“You get such satisfaction out of teasing me, don’t you?”<br />“I still maintain that you like it.”<br /><br />Fabulous read. One click it and read it. <br /></b></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer804092127" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10103647921323893989">5 stars<br/><br/><a href='http://s1274.photobucket.com/albums/y432/RReadoholic/?action=view&current=PhotoGrid_1388404923882_zps406faf91.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388418812i/7830216._SY540_.jpg' width='390' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>The Grand Master recruits new vampires. Among them is a female vampire, Sam. Jared isn't too happy about it. Sexist or what?!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Why did disputing get this bloke horny?</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I love the push and pull in the story and not 'insta love->sex->I love you'. I was a bit bored with the training/coaching but otherwise I was gripped. Great <b>sexual tension</b> and love the<b> banter.</b> <br/><br/>My third Suzanne Wright book and it was another hit. I<b> love the characters </b>she creates, the sex scenes was <b>smoking hot </b>a</span>
  <span id="freeText10103647921323893989" style="display:none">5 stars<br><br><a href="http://s1274.photobucket.com/albums/y432/RReadoholic/?action=view&amp;current=PhotoGrid_1388404923882_zps406faf91.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388418812i/7830216._SY540_.jpg" width="390" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The Grand Master recruits new vampires. Among them is a female vampire, Sam. Jared isn't too happy about it. Sexist or what?!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Why did disputing get this bloke horny?</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I love the push and pull in the story and not 'insta love-&gt;sex-&gt;I love you'. I was a bit bored with the training/coaching but otherwise I was gripped. Great <b>sexual tension</b> and love the<b> banter.</b> <br><br>My third Suzanne Wright book and it was another hit. I<b> love the characters </b>she creates, the sex scenes was <b>smoking hot </b>and I <b>love her writing style.</b><br><br>If that's not enough motivation to give this a go, meet Jared:<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Once won't be enough. I want to do it over, and over, and over, and over again.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('XZyvD9yvenfV9wbVRRQ5WUMPVrvpGvNTI4KtSGRTqVfOP6hLQStKSmF0YEydUG2rton60uby9MgCT27ki9A++Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('1aUAsRU56cx2YxMcAAQ+TqdJii32fwjwXw9emAojqslGBgf1iL3Z8cLgdYXYQGq8Us8mRPmXD2t+wp005aA9Zw==')})
  }
//]]>
